performance and identifying opportunities of improvement. this report contains consolidated

activities
founded on september 13, 1973 in eastern minas gerais, celulose nipo-brasileira s.a.
(cenibra) is a privately held company controlled by japan brazil paper and pulp resources
development co., ltd. (jbp). the main shareholders of jpb are oji holdings corporation and
itochu corporation.

cenibra‚Äôs industrial plant is located in belo oriente, state of minas gerais. it comprises
[^vislhjolkzovy[√§ilyl\jhs`w[\zw\swwyvk\j[pvuspulz^p[oh[v[hspuz[hsslkjhwhjp[`vm
1.19 million tons/year and three regional forest stewardship units in the state of minas gerais
(guanh√£es, nova era and rio doce). moreover, it has a dedicated port terminal in barra do
9phjov,:pu^opjop[ovskzh pu[lylz[hukhjvywvyh[lhukjvttlyjphsv…âjlpu)lsv
horizonte.

cenibra ships 95% of its production to foreign markets, mainly asia, europe and north
(tlypjh+pz[ypi\[pvujlu[lyzhukylwylzlu[h[pvu zhslzv…âjlzhyllz[hispzolkpu[olzlhylhz
to meet the customers‚Äô requirements.

the industrial plant is supplied with wood from the company‚Äôs own lands and leased lands,
as well as from small farmers that plant eucalyptus under a forestation incentive arrangement
(the latter answered for 21% of the plant‚Äôs wood consumption in 2014). cenibra‚Äôs foresta-
tion incentive program is implemented in 88 municipalities in the state of minas gerais. with
a headcount of 7,648 employees and contractors‚Äô personnel, the company operates in 54
municipalities, where it is engaged in several social and environmental projects, partnerships
with local entities and other integration and income-generating initiatives with an aim to sup-
port the region‚Äôs sustainable development.

ethical principles and code of conduct
cenibra‚Äôs code of conduct is the main directive applicable to the company‚Äôs relationship
with its stakeholders. revised in 2014, the code sets forth recommendations and guiding
principles with respect to employee attitude, commercial relations with customers and sup-
pliers, relationship with a number of entities and the community, and guidelines relative to
myh\k jvyy\w[pvu npm[z huk jvu√•pj[z vm pu[lylz[ htvun v[oly [opunz (ptpun h[ l…âlj[p]ls`
implementing the code and reinforcing the need for compliance and misconduct prevention,
cenibra provides periodical institutional training to all the personnel, on which occasion
kv\i[zhyljshyp√§lkhukz\nnlz[pvuzhukjyp[pjpztzhyljvtwpslk0uhss[olul^s`opylk
employees were given the corresponding training.

cenibra makes use of an internal ombudsman arrangement as the main communication
channel to receive complaints. this system is controlled by the ethics committee coordinator,
who is in charge of receiving eventual complaints related to ethical issues and submitting them
to the remaining committee members. the committee is responsible for reviewing and check-
ing possible violations and complaints, ensuring uniform criteria when evaluating the cases,
and caring for proper personal and professional conduct of employees and business partners.
the committee makes recommendations to and supports the executive management. the
external ombudsman service takes the form of a toll-free telephone (talk to cenibra) that
ensures anonymity to complainants, if so requested.

of business sustainability.



environmental recovery

cenibra invests in the protection, conservation and improvement of the existing protected
areas in its lands. the improvement actions, also known as forest restoration, include planting
native trees and removing eucalyptus trees so as to create a forest cover consisting solely of
native species. in 2014, such actions resulted in 50,000 tree seedlings planted over an area
of 283 hectares. on the other hand, eucalyptus trees were removed from a total area of 392
hectares, so that the native forest cover can regenerate.



biodiversity

biodiversity conservation and protection are some of cenibra‚Äôs sustainability strategy prior-
ities. the company‚Äôs biodiversity asset consists of 104,000 hectares of forests that sustain a
varied wildlife and abundant water resources, and cenibra is engaged in several initiatives in
line with its integrated management policy to preserve it. guidelines and goals are one of the
references for the development of environmental projects to monitor and improve the com-
pany‚Äôs environmental performance, as well as to ensure that the necessary resources will be
